 </P>  <P STYLE="margin-top:24pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>GOLDMAN SACHS COMMODITY STRATEGY FUND </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>a series of </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>GOLDMAN
SACHS TRUST </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">71 South Wacker Drive </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">Chicago, Illinois 60606 </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="right">August&nbsp;19, 2020 </P>  <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Dear
Shareholder:&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </P>  <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">You are cordially invited to attend a Special Meeting of Shareholders (the &#147;Meeting&#148;)
of the Goldman Sachs Commodity Strategy Fund (the &#147;Commodity Strategy Fund&#148; or &#147;Fund&#148;), a series of the Goldman Sachs Trust (the &#147;Trust&#148;), to be held on November&nbsp;13, 2020, at 10:00 a.m. (Eastern time). The Meeting
will be conducted as a virtual meeting hosted by means of a live webcast. The Board of Trustees of the Trust has implemented a virtual meeting format primarily to reflect our and global concerns regarding the spread
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">of&nbsp;COVID-19.&nbsp;Shareholders</FONT> will be able to listen, vote, and submit questions from their home or any location with internet connectivity. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">You or your proxyholder will be able to attend the Meeting online, vote and submit questions by visiting
https://viewproxy.com/GoldmanSachsCommodityStrategyFund/broadridgevsm/ and using a control number assigned by Broadridge Financial Solutions, Inc. To register and receive access to the virtual meeting, you will need to follow the instructions
provided in the Notice of Special Meeting and Proxy Statement that follow. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">At this important meeting, you will be asked to consider and
act upon the following proposals. Each proposal is to be voted upon only by Shareholders of the Commodity Strategy Fund: </P> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE CELLSPACING="0" CELLPADDING="0" WIDTH="100%" BORDER="0" STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" ALIGN="center">


<TR>

<TD WIDTH="11%"></TD>

<TD VALIGN="bottom" WIDTH="1%"></TD>
<TD WIDTH="88%"></TD></TR>


<TR STYLE="page-break-inside:avoid ; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">
<TD VALIGN="top"><B>Proposal&nbsp;1.</B></TD>
<TD VALIGN="bottom">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD VALIGN="top"><B>To approve a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">sub-advisory</FONT> agreement for the Fund between Goldman Sachs Asset Management, L.P. (the &#147;Investment Adviser&#148;) and CoreCommodity Management, LLC
(&#147;CoreCommodity&#148;).</B></TD></TR>
<TR STYLE="font-size:1pt">
<TD HEIGHT="13"></TD>
<TD HEIGHT="13" COLSPAN="2"></TD></TR>
<TR STYLE="page-break-inside:avoid ; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">
<TD VALIGN="top"><B>Proposal 2.</B></TD>
<TD VALIGN="bottom">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD VALIGN="top"><B>To approve the use of a &#147;manager of managers&#148; structure whereby the Board of Trustees and the Investment Adviser would be authorized to hire and replace investment <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">sub-advisers</FONT> on
behalf of the Fund without Shareholder approval.</B></TD></TR>
<TR STYLE="font-size:1pt">
<TD HEIGHT="13"></TD>
<TD HEIGHT="13" COLSPAN="2"></TD></TR>
<TR STYLE="page-break-inside:avoid ; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">
<TD VALIGN="top"><B>Proposal 3.</B></TD>
<TD VALIGN="bottom">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD VALIGN="top"><B>To transact such other business as may properly come before the Meeting or any postponement or adjournment thereof.</B></TD></TR>
</TABLE>    <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">A formal Notice of Special Meeting and Proxy Statement setting forth in detail the matters to
come before the Meeting are attached to this letter, and a proxy card is enclosed for your use. You should read the Proxy Statement carefully. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>WHETHER OR NOT YOU PLAN TO BE PRESENT AT THE MEETING, YOUR VOTE IS VERY IMPORTANT.</B> The Board of Trustees of the Trust unanimously
recommends that you vote &#147;FOR&#148; each proposal. However, before you vote, please read the Proxy Statement for a complete description of the proposals. If you do not plan to be present at the Meeting, you can vote by signing, dating and
returning the enclosed proxy card promptly or by using the Internet or telephone voting options as described on your proxy card. If you have </P>

 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">2 </P>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>Important Information to Help You Understand and Vote on the Proposals &#150; Questions and
Answers </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The following questions and answers provide an overview of the matters on which you are being asked to vote. The accompanying Proxy Statement
contains more detailed information about each proposal, and we encourage you to read it in its entirety before voting. <B>Your vote is important. </B> </P> <P STYLE="font-size:18pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><B>Q:</B></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left"><B></B><B><I>What is the purpose of this proxy solicitation?</I></B><B> </B></P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">A:</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">The purpose of this proxy solicitation is to ask Shareholders of the Commodity Strategy Fund to
(i)&nbsp;approve a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">sub-advisory</FONT> agreement for the Fund between the Investment Adviser and CoreCommodity and (ii)&nbsp;approve the use of a &#147;manager of managers&#148; structure whereby the Board of
Trustees and the Investment Adviser would be authorized to hire and replace investment <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">sub-advisers</FONT> on behalf of the Fund without Shareholder approval. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>QUESTIONS SPECIFIC TO THE PROPOSALS </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>PROPOSAL 1
</B>&#151; <B>TO APPROVE A <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">SUB-ADVISORY</FONT> AGREEMENT. </B> </P> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><B>Q:</B></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left"><B></B><B><I>Why am I being asked to approve a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">sub-advisory</FONT> agreement
for the Fund?</I></B><B> </B></P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">A:</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">The Commodity Strategy Fund seeks to maintain substantial economic exposure to the performance of the
commodities markets. In pursuing its objective, the Fund attempts to provide long and/or short exposure to the returns of real assets that trade in the commodity markets without direct investment in physical commodities. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">GSAM believes that CoreCommodity&#146;s experience investing in the commodities markets and long-term track record of performance present a
positive opportunity for the Fund. Given the Fund&#146;s investment focus of maintaining substantial economic exposure to the performance of the commodities markets, GSAM believes hiring an investment manager that specializes in investing in the
commodities market, subject to GSAM&#146;s oversight, would be beneficial to Shareholders. CoreCommodity is an independent commodity asset management firm that provides advisory and fiduciary management services to investors globally, with
approximately $3.2&nbsp;billion in assets across long-only and absolute return commodity investment programs as of June&nbsp;30, 2020. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The Investment Company Act of 1940 Act generally requires that any investment management agreement, including any <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">sub-advisory</FONT> agreement, be approved by the affirmative vote of a majority of the outstanding shares of the Fund. Accordingly, Shareholders of the Fund are being asked to approve the proposed <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">sub-advisory</FONT> agreement. The <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">sub-advisory</FONT> agreement with CoreCommodity was unanimously approved by the Trustees present at a meeting held on July&nbsp;23, 2020. Although one
Trustee was unable to attend this meeting, that Trustee supported the Proposal. </P>  <P STYLE="font-size:18pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><B>Q:</B></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left"><B></B><B><I>Will the proposed <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">sub-advisory</FONT> agreement with
CoreCommodity change how the Fund is managed?</I></B><B> </B></P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">A:</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">If approved, the Fund&#146;s benchmark would change from the S&amp;P GSCI Total Return Index to the Bloomberg
Commodity Total Return Index, which is more widely used as a commodity benchmark. Although CoreCommodity has a different investment philosophy and employs different investment techniques, it is not anticipated that the proposed <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">sub-advisory</FONT> agreement with CoreCommodity<B><I> </I></B>will result in any material changes to the principal investment strategies of the Fund. For example, CoreCommodity will take various factors into account when
seeking commodity market exposure, such as, without limitation, the results of proprietary models developed by CoreCommodity, relative price differentials for various commodity futures for current delivery as compared to those for future delivery,
and market conditions. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:18pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><B>Q:</B></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left"><B></B><B><I>Will the proposed <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">sub-advisory</FONT> agreement with
CoreCommodity increase the fees that I will pay?</I></B><B> </B></P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">A:</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">No, it is not anticipated that the proposed <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">sub-advisory</FONT> agreement with
CoreCommodity<B><I> </I></B>will result in any changes to fees that you will pay. The Investment Adviser is responsible for paying any fees due to CoreCommodity under the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">sub-advisory</FONT> agreement.
</P></TD></TR></TABLE>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P>  <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">3 </P>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>PROPOSAL 2 </B>&#151; <B>TO APPROVE A &#147;MANAGER OF MANAGERS&#148; STRUCTURE. </B> </P>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><B>Q:</B></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left"><B></B><B><I>Why am I being asked to approve the use of a &#147;manager of managers&#148; structure?</I></B><B>
</B></P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">A:</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">Shareholders of the Fund are being asked to approve the use of a &#147;manager of managers&#148; structure that
would permit the Investment Adviser, subject to approval by the Board of Trustees, to hire and replace investment <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">sub-advisers</FONT> for the Fund without obtaining prior Shareholder approval (the &#147;Manager of
Managers Structure&#148;). The Manager of Managers Structure would enable the Fund to operate with greater efficiency in the future by allowing the Fund to utilize <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">sub-advisers</FONT> best suited to its needs without
incurring the expense and potential delays that could be associated with obtaining Shareholder approvals. Without the Manager of Managers Structure, Shareholders of the Fund would have to vote to approve any new
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">sub-adviser,</FONT> though the Investment Adviser could terminate a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">sub-adviser</FONT> without shareholder approval. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The Investment Adviser has received an exemptive order from the U.S. Securities and Exchange Commission (the &#147;SEC&#148;) permitting the
use of the Manager of Managers Structure. In order for the Fund to rely on the Manager of Managers Structure, it must be approved by the affirmative vote of a majority of the outstanding shares of the Fund. The Manager of Managers Structure was
unanimously approved by the Trustees at a meeting held on July&nbsp;23, 2020. Although one Trustee was unable to attend this meeting, that Trustee supported the Proposal. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>GENERAL QUESTIONS </B></P> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><B>Q:</B></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left"><B></B><B><I>What happens if Shareholders do not approve one or more of the Proposals?</I></B><B>
</B></P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">A:</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">If Shareholders do not approve one or more of the Proposals, the Board of Trustees will take such actions as it
deems necessary or appropriate in the best interests of the Fund&#146;s Shareholders based on the facts and circumstances. The approval of one Proposal is not contingent on the approval of another (<I>i.e.</I>, Proposal 1 is not contingent on the
approval of Proposal 2 and vice versa). </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:18pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><B>Q.</B></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left"><B></B><B><I>Will my vote make a difference?</I></B><B> </B></P></TD></TR></TABLE>

toll-free number on your enclosed proxy card, in each case using the voting control number that appears on your proxy card. However, whichever method you choose, please take the time to read the Proxy Statement before you vote. </P>

Goldman Sachs Commodity Strategy Fund (the &#147;Commodity Strategy Fund&#148; or &#147;Fund&#148;): </P>  <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">A Special Meeting of
Shareholders (the &#147;Meeting&#148;) of the Commodity Strategy Fund, a series of the Goldman Sachs Trust (the &#147;Trust&#148;), will be held virtually on November&nbsp;13, 2020, at 10:00 a.m. (Eastern time), by means of a live webcast, for the
following purposes. </P>  <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Each proposal is to be voted upon only by Shareholders of the Fund: </P>
<P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

your shares electronically. To participate in the Meeting, Shareholders must register in advance by visiting <B>https://viewproxy.com/GoldmanSachsCommodityStrategyFund/broadridgevsm/</B> and submitting the required information to Broadridge
Financial Solutions, Inc. (&#147;Broadridge&#148;), the Fund&#146;s proxy tabulator. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Shareholders whose shares are registered directly
with the Fund in the Shareholder&#146;s name will be asked to submit their name and control number found on the Shareholder&#146;s proxy card in order to register to participate in and vote at the Meeting. Shareholders whose shares are held by a
broker, bank or other nominee must first obtain a &#147;legal proxy&#148; from the applicable nominee/record holder, who will then provide the Shareholder with a newly-issued control number. We note that obtaining a legal proxy may take several
days. Requests for registration should be received no later than 5:00 p.m., Eastern Time, on November&nbsp;12, 2020, but in any event must be received by the scheduled time for commencement of the Meeting. Once Shareholders have obtained a new
control number, they must visit <B>https://viewproxy.com/GoldmanSachsCommodityStrategyFund/broadridgevsm/</B> and submit their name and newly issued control number in order to register to participate in and vote at the Meeting. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">1 </P>

Broadridge that confirms that their registration request has been received and is under review by Broadridge. Once a Shareholder&#146;s registration request has been accepted, the Shareholder will receive (i)&nbsp;an email containing an event link
and <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">dial-in</FONT> information to attend the Meeting, and (ii)&nbsp;an email with a password to enter at the event link in order to access the Meeting. <B>Shareholders may vote before or during the Meeting at
https://viewproxy.com/GoldmanSachsCommodityStrategyFund/broadridgevsm/.</B> Only Shareholders of the Fund present virtually or by proxy will be able to vote, or otherwise exercise the powers of a Shareholder, at the Meeting. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The Meeting webcast will begin promptly at 10:00 a.m. (Eastern time). We encourage you to access the Meeting prior to the start time. For
additional information on how you can attend and participate in the virtual Meeting, please see the instructions beginning on page 6 of the proxy statement that follows. Because the Meeting will be a completely virtual meeting, there will be no
physical location for Shareholders to attend. </P>  <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The matters referred to above are discussed in the Proxy Statement attached to this
Notice. Shareholders of record at the close of business on August&nbsp;17, 2020, the record date for the Meeting, are entitled to receive notice of and to vote at the Meeting and at any postponements or adjournments thereof. <B>If you will not be
present at the Meeting, we urge you to sign, date and promptly return the enclosed proxy card in the envelope provided, which is addressed for your convenience and needs no postage if mailed in the United States. You may also vote easily and quickly
by Internet or by telephone. In order to avoid further solicitation and reduce unnecessary costs, we ask your cooperation in returning your proxy promptly. </B> </P>

<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">You may revoke your proxy at any time at or before the Meeting, by submitting to the Secretary of the Trust at the Trust&#146;s principal executive offices a
written notice of revocation or subsequently executed proxy or by attending the virtual Meeting and electing to vote. </P>

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>INSTRUCTIONS FOR SIGNING PROXY CARDS </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The following general guidelines for signing proxy cards may be of assistance to you and will help avoid the time and expense to the Investment Adviser
involved in validating your vote if you fail to sign your proxy card properly. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">1. <B>Individual Accounts: </B>Sign your name exactly as it appears in the
registration on the proxy card. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">2. <B>Joint Accounts: </B>Either party may sign, but the name of the party signing should conform exactly to the name
shown in the registration on the proxy card. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">3. <B>All Other Accounts: </B>The capacity of the individual signing the proxy card should be indicated
unless it is reflected in the form of registration. For example: </P> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<IMG SRC="g93780g13n02.jpg" ALT="LOGO">
 </P>  <P STYLE="margin-top:24pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B><A NAME="toc_def93780_1"></A>SPECIAL MEETING </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>OF </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>GOLDMAN SACHS
COMMODITY STRATEGY FUND </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>a series of </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>GOLDMAN SACHS TRUST </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">71
South Wacker Drive </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">Chicago, Illinois 60606 </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>PROXY STATEMENT </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="right">August&nbsp;19, 2020 </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">This Proxy
Statement is furnished in connection with the solicitation of proxies by and on behalf of the Board of Trustees of the Goldman Sachs Trust (the &#147;Trust&#148;) for use at the Special Meeting of Shareholders of the Goldman Sachs Commodity Strategy
Fund (the &#147;Commodity Strategy Fund&#148; or &#147;Fund&#148;) to be held virtually on November&nbsp;13, 2020, at 10:00 a.m. (Eastern time), or any postponement or adjournment thereof, for the purposes set forth in the accompanying Notice of
Special Meeting. Such meeting and any postponement or adjournment thereof is referred to as the &#147;Meeting.&#148; This Proxy Statement, the accompanying Notice of Special Meeting, and the accompanying proxy card are being mailed to Shareholders
on or about August&nbsp;27, 2020. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The Meeting will be a virtual meeting conducted exclusively via live webcast starting at 10:00 a.m.
(Eastern time). You will be able to attend the Meeting online, submit your questions during the Meeting and vote your shares electronically. To participate in the Meeting, Shareholders must register in advance by visiting
<B>https://viewproxy.com/GoldmanSachsCommodityStrategyFund/broadridgevsm/</B> and submitting the required information to Broadridge Financial Solutions, Inc. (&#147;Broadridge&#148;), the Fund&#146;s proxy tabulator. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Shareholders whose shares are registered directly with the Fund in the Shareholder&#146;s name will be asked to submit their name and control
number found on the Shareholder&#146;s proxy card in order to register to participate in and vote at the Meeting. Shareholders whose shares are held by a broker, bank or other nominee must first obtain a &#147;legal proxy&#148; from the applicable
nominee/record holder, who will then provide the Shareholder with a newly-issued control number. We note that obtaining a legal proxy may take several days. Requests for registration should be received no later than 5:00 p.m., Eastern Time, on
November&nbsp;12, 2020, but in any event must be received by the scheduled time for commencement of the Meeting. Once Shareholders have obtained a new control number, they must visit
<B>https://viewproxy.com/GoldmanSachsCommodityStrategyFund/broadridgevsm/</B> and submit their name and newly issued control number in order to register to participate in and vote at the Meeting. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">After Shareholders have submitted their registration information, they will receive an email from Broadridge that confirms that their
registration request has been received and is under review by Broadridge. Once a Shareholder&#146;s registration request has been accepted, the Shareholder will receive (i)&nbsp;an email containing an event link and
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">dial-in</FONT> information to attend the Meeting, and (ii)&nbsp;an email with a password to enter at the event link in order to access the Meeting. <B>Shareholders may vote before or during the Meeting at
https://viewproxy.com/GoldmanSachsCommodityStrategyFund/broadridgevsm/.</B> Only Shareholders of the Fund present virtually or by proxy will be able to vote, or otherwise exercise the powers of a Shareholder, at the Meeting. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P>  <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">6 </P>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">In light of the rapidly changing developments related to
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">coronavirus&nbsp;(COVID-19),&nbsp;we</FONT> are pleased to offer our Shareholders a completely virtual Meeting, which provides worldwide access and communication, while protecting the health and safety of our
Shareholders, Trustees and management. We are committed to ensuring that Shareholders will be afforded the same rights and opportunities to participate as they would at <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">an&nbsp;in-person&nbsp;meeting.</FONT> We will
try to answer as many Shareholder-submitted questions as time permits that comply with the Meeting rules of conduct. However, we reserve the right to edit profanity or other inappropriate language, or to exclude questions that are not pertinent to
meeting matters or that are otherwise inappropriate. If substantially similar questions are received, we will group such questions together and provide a single response to avoid repetition. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The Trustees have fixed the close of business on August&nbsp;17, 2020 as the record date for the determination of Shareholders entitled to
notice of, and to vote at, the Meeting (the &#147;Record Date&#148;). Shareholders of record of the Fund on the Record Date are entitled to one vote per share at the Meeting. <U>Exhibit A</U> to this Proxy Statement sets forth the number of shares
of beneficial interest of the Fund outstanding as of the Record Date. <U>Exhibit B</U> to this Proxy Statement sets forth the persons who owned beneficially more than 5% of any class of the Fund as of July&nbsp;16, 2020. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The Trust&#146;s officers, and personnel of Goldman Sachs Asset Management, L.P. (the &#147;Investment Adviser&#148; or &#147;GSAM&#148;), the
Fund&#146;s investment adviser, and the Fund&#146;s transfer agent and any authorized proxy solicitation agent, may also solicit proxies by telephone, facsimile, Internet or in person. If the Trust records votes through the Internet or by telephone,
it will use procedures designed to authenticate Shareholders&#146; identities, to allow Shareholders to authorize the voting of their shares in accordance with their instructions, and to confirm that their identities have been properly recorded.
</P>  <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The Trust has engaged Broadridge, an independent proxy solicitation firm, to assist in the distribution of the proxy materials and
the solicitation and tabulation of proxies.&nbsp;The cost of Broadridge&#146;s services with respect to the Trust, which will be borne by GSAM, is estimated to be approximately $212,986, plus reasonable <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">out-of-pocket</FONT></FONT> expenses. </P>  <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">To vote by mail, sign, date and promptly return the enclosed proxy
card in the accompanying postage <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">pre-paid</FONT> envelope. To vote by Internet or telephone, please use the control number on your proxy card and follow the instructions as described on your proxy card. If you have
any questions regarding the proxy materials, please contact Broadridge at <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">800-574-5796.</FONT></FONT> <B>If the enclosed proxy card is properly executed and received prior to the
Meeting and has not been revoked, the shares represented thereby will be voted in accordance with the instructions marked on the returned proxy card or, if no instructions are marked on the returned proxy card, the proxy card will be voted
&#147;FOR&#148; Proposal 1 and Proposal 2, and voted in the discretion of the persons named as proxies in connection with any other matter that may properly come before the Meeting or any adjournment(s) or postponement(s) thereof. </B> </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Any person giving a proxy may revoke it at any time before it is exercised by submitting to the Secretary of the Trust at the Trust&#146;s
principal executive offices a written notice of revocation or subsequently executed proxy or by attending the virtual Meeting and voting during the webcast. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">If (i)&nbsp;you are a member of a household in which multiple Shareholders of the Fund share the same address, (ii)&nbsp;your shares are held
in &#147;street name&#148; and (iii)&nbsp;your broker or bank has received consent to household material, then your broker or bank may have sent to your household only one copy of this Proxy Statement, unless your broker or bank previously received
contrary instructions from a Shareholder in your household. If you are part of a household that has received only one copy of this Proxy Statement, the Trust will deliver promptly a separate copy of this Proxy Statement to you upon written or oral
request. To receive a separate copy of this Proxy Statement, please contact the Trust by calling toll free <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">1-800-621-2550</FONT></FONT></FONT> (for
institutional shareholders) or <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">1-800-526-7384</FONT></FONT></FONT> (for retail shareholders), or by mail at Goldman Sachs Funds, P.O. Box 06050,
Chicago, Illinois 60606-6306. If your shares are held with certain banks, trust companies, brokers, registered </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P>  <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">7 </P>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">
investment advisers and other financial intermediaries&nbsp;(each, an &#147;Authorized Institution&#148;) and you would like to receive a separate copy of future proxy statements, notices of
internet availability of proxy materials, prospectuses or annual reports or you are now receiving multiple copies of these documents and would like to receive a single copy in the future, please contact your Authorized Institution. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:24pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>IMPORTANT NOTICE REGARDING THE AVAILABILITY OF PROXY MATERIALS FOR THE SPECIAL MEETING TO BE HELD ON NOVEMBER&nbsp;13, 2020 </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">This Proxy Statement is available online at&nbsp;https://viewproxy.com/GoldmanSachsCommodityStrategyFund/broadridgevsm/&nbsp;(please have the
control number found on your proxy card ready when you visit this website). <B>IN ADDITION, COPIES OF THE FUND&#146;S MOST </B><B>RECENT ANNUAL AND SEMI-ANNUAL REPORT, INCLUDING FINANCIAL STATEMENTS, HAVE PREVIOUSLY BEEN MAILED TO SHAREHOLDERS.
COPIES OF THE FUND&#146;S MOST RECENT ANNUAL AND SEMI-ANNUAL REPORT, INCLUDING FINANCIAL STATEMENTS, ARE ALSO AVAILABLE AT WWW.GSAMFUNDS.COM/MUTUALFUNDS. THE TRUST WILL FURNISH TO ANY SHAREHOLDER UPON REQUEST, WITHOUT CHARGE, AN ADDITIONAL COPY OF
THE FUND&#146;S MOST RECENT ANNUAL REPORT AND SUBSEQUENT SEMI-ANNUAL REPORT TO SHAREHOLDERS. ANNUAL REPORTS AND SEMI-ANNUAL REPORTS TO SHAREHOLDERS MAY BE OBTAINED BY WRITING TO: GOLDMAN SACHS TRUST, P.O. BOX 06050, CHICAGO, ILLINOIS 60606-6306; OR
BY TELEPHONE TOLL-FREE AT: <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">1-800-621-2550</FONT></FONT></FONT> (FOR INSTITUTIONAL SHAREHOLDERS) AND <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">1-800-526-7384</FONT></FONT></FONT> (FOR RETAIL SHAREHOLDERS).</B> </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P>  <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">8 </P>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B><A NAME="toc_def93780_2"></A>PROPOSAL 1 </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>TO APPROVE A <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">SUB-ADVISORY</FONT> AGREEMENT FOR THE FUND BETWEEN GOLDMAN SACHS ASSET MANAGEMENT, L.P. AND
CORECOMMODITY MANAGEMENT, LLC </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Introduction: </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Shareholders of the Goldman Sachs Commodity Strategy Fund (the &#147;Commodity Strategy Fund&#148; or &#147;Fund&#148;) are being asked to
approve an investment <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">sub-advisory</FONT> agreement (the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">&#147;Sub-Advisory</FONT> Agreement&#148;) between Goldman Sachs Asset Management, L.P. (the &#147;Investment Adviser&#148; or
&#147;GSAM&#148;) and CoreCommodity Management, LLC (&#147;CoreCommodity&#148;) with respect to the Fund. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The Commodity Strategy Fund
seeks to maintain substantial economic exposure to the performance of the commodities markets. In pursuing its objective, the Fund attempts to provide long and/or short exposure to the returns of real assets that trade in the commodity markets
without direct investment in physical commodities. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">As discussed further below, CoreCommodity is an independent commodity asset management
firm that provides advisory and fiduciary commodity management services to investors globally, with approximately $3.2&nbsp;billion in assets across long-only and absolute return commodity investment programs as of June&nbsp;30, 2020.
CoreCommodity&#146;s strategy seeks to provide diversified and unlevered global commodity exposure through a diversified portfolio of commodity futures-related investments. GSAM believes that CoreCommodity&#146;s experience investing in the
commodities markets and long-term track record of performance present a positive opportunity for the Fund. Given the Fund&#146;s investment focus of maintaining substantial economic exposure to the performance of the commodities markets, GSAM
believes hiring an investment manager that specializes in investing in the commodities market, subject to GSAM&#146;s oversight, would be beneficial to Shareholders. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">If approved, the Fund&#146;s benchmark would change from the S&amp;P GSCI Total Return Index to the Bloomberg Commodity Total Return Index
(&#147;BCOM&#148;), which is more widely used as a commodity benchmark. The majority of the funds in the Commodities Broad Basket and Commodities Focused Morningstar categories use BCOM as their benchmark (77% of funds and 81% of assets). The key
differences in the benchmarks are the weights to Energy and Precious Metals. Although CoreCommodity has a different investment philosophy and employs different investment techniques, it is not anticipated that the proposed <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">sub-advisory</FONT> agreement with CoreCommodity<B><I> </I></B>will result in any material changes to the principal investment strategies of the Fund. For example, CoreCommodity will take various factors into account when
seeking commodity market exposure, such as, without limitation, the results of proprietary models developed by CoreCommodity, relative price differentials for various commodity futures for current delivery as compared to those for future delivery,
and market conditions. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">If approved by Shareholders at the Meeting, the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Sub-Advisory</FONT> Agreement
will take effect on or around November&nbsp;30, 2020. <B><I>Approval of the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Sub-Advisory</FONT> Agreement is not expected to result in any increase in investment advisory fees or overall operating expenses with
respect to the Commodity Strategy Fund.</I></B> </P>  <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The Investment Company Act of 1940 Act (the &#147;1940 Act&#148;) generally requires
that any investment management agreement, including any <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">sub-advisory</FONT> agreement, be approved by the affirmative vote of a majority of the outstanding shares of the Fund. Accordingly, Shareholders of the Fund
are being asked to approve the proposed <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Sub-Advisory</FONT> Agreement. The proposed <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Sub-Advisory</FONT> Agreement, a form of which is attached as <U>Exhibit C,</U> was unanimously
approved by the Trustees present at a meeting held on July&nbsp;23, 2020. Although one Trustee was unable to attend this meeting, that Trustee supported the Proposal. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Proposed <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Sub-Advisory</FONT> Agreement with CoreCommodity: </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Under the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">proposed&nbsp;Sub-Advisory&nbsp;Agreement,</FONT> subject to the supervision and oversight of GSAM,
CoreCommodity agrees to provide the Fund with investment research, advice and supervision and furnish a </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P>  <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">9 </P>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">
continuous investment program for, and manage the investment and reinvestment of, the Fund&#146;s assets (or a portion thereof). CoreCommodity determines in its discretion the securities, cash
and other financial instruments to be purchased, retained or sold for the Fund within the parameters of the investment approach, policies, restrictions and guidelines applicable to the Fund as provided by GSAM, the provisions of <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">the&nbsp;Sub-Advisory&nbsp;Agreement,</FONT> all applicable laws, rules and regulations and the Fund&#146;s registration statement on <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Form&nbsp;N-1A&nbsp;under</FONT> the 1940 Act. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Under <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">the&nbsp;Sub-Advisory&nbsp;Agreement,</FONT> CoreCommodity agrees to pay for all expenses incurred by
it in connection with its services to the Fund. As compensation for its services, CoreCommodity is entitled to receive fees from GSAM (not the Fund) each calendar quarter based on an annual percentage of the average daily net assets of the Fund. The
annual percentage is determined based on breakpoints calculated&nbsp;according to the following schedule: </P> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE CELLSPACING="0" CELLPADDING="0" WIDTH="68%" BORDER="0" STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" ALIGN="center">

</TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">The&nbsp;Sub-Advisory&nbsp;Agreement</FONT> will remain in effect for two
years after its effective date and will continue thereafter for successive periods of twelve months, provided that its continuance is approved at least annually (i)&nbsp;by the vote of a majority of those Trustees of the Trust who are not parties to
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">the&nbsp;Sub-Advisory&nbsp;Agreement</FONT> or interested persons of any such party, cast in person at a meeting called for the purpose of voting on such approval, and (ii)&nbsp;by either the vote of (A)&nbsp;the
Board or (B)&nbsp;a majority of the outstanding voting securities of the Fund (within the meaning of the 1940 Act). </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">The&nbsp;Sub-Advisory&nbsp;Agreement</FONT> provides for termination, without payment of any penalty, (i)&nbsp;by vote of a majority of the Board or by a vote of a majority of the outstanding voting securities of the Fund,
(ii)&nbsp;by GSAM on not less than 60 days&#146; written notice to CoreCommodity (or immediately in the event of a material breach by CoreCommodity), or (iii)&nbsp;by CoreCommodity on not less than 90 days&#146; written notice to GSAM and the Trust.
Notwithstanding the above, CoreCommodity may not terminate <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">the&nbsp;Sub-Advisory&nbsp;Agreement</FONT> during <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">the&nbsp;24-month&nbsp;period</FONT> immediately following the effective
date of <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">the&nbsp;Sub-Advisory&nbsp;Agreement</FONT> with respect to the Fund. <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">The&nbsp;Sub-Advisory&nbsp;Agreement</FONT> shall automatically terminate in the event of its assignment
or the assignment of the Fund&#146;s management agreement with GSAM. <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">The&nbsp;Sub-Advisory&nbsp;Agreement</FONT> shall also terminate in the event that the Fund&#146;s management agreement with GSAM is terminated.
</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Trustees&#146; Considerations: </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">At a meeting held on July&nbsp;23, 2020, based upon their review, and after consideration of such factors and information they considered
relevant, the Trustees present at the meeting, including those Trustees of the Trust who are not deemed to be &#147;interested persons&#148; (as defined in the 1940 Act) of the Trust (the &#147;Independent Trustees&#148;), unanimously approved the <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Sub-Advisory</FONT> Agreement and voted to recommend to Shareholders that they approve Proposal 1. Although one Trustee was unable to attend this meeting, that Trustee supported the Proposal. In connection with the
July&nbsp;23, 2020 meeting, the Board and the Independent Trustees received written materials and oral presentations on the topics covered, and were advised by their independent legal counsel. In addition, CoreCommodity provided information in
response to a request from the Investment Adviser. For more information on the factors considered by the Board, please see the sections immediately below. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><I>Nature, Extent and Quality of the Services to be Provided Under
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">the&nbsp;Sub-Advisory&nbsp;Agreement</FONT> </I></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">In evaluating
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">the&nbsp;Sub-Advisory&nbsp;Agreement,</FONT> the Trustees present at the July&nbsp;23, 2020 meeting relied on the information provided by GSAM and CoreCommodity.&nbsp;In evaluating the nature, extent and quality of
services to be provided by CoreCommodity under the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Sub-Advisory&nbsp;Agreement,&nbsp;the</FONT> Trustees considered information about </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P>  <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">10 </P>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">
CoreCommodity&#146;s&nbsp;(i)&nbsp;personnel and its compensation structure; (ii)&nbsp;track record in managing other client accounts with investment strategies similar to those to be employed on
behalf of the Fund; (iii)&nbsp;policies and procedures in place to address potential conflicts of interest; and (iv)&nbsp;compliance program and code of ethics. In this regard, they considered assessments provided by GSAM of CoreCommodity,
CoreCommodity&#146;s&nbsp;investment strategies and personnel, and its compliance program. The Trustees also considered that CoreCommodity currently manages other assets for clients of an affiliate of GSAM. They noted that, because CoreCommodity had
not previously provided services to the Fund, there was no performance information to evaluate with respect to the Fund. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><I>Costs of
Services to be Provided </I></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The Trustees reviewed the terms of
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">the&nbsp;Sub-Advisory&nbsp;Agreement</FONT> and the proposed fee schedule, which included breakpoints. They noted that the compensation paid to CoreCommodity would be paid by GSAM, not by the Fund. They also noted
that the terms of <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">the&nbsp;Sub-Advisory&nbsp;Agreement</FONT> were the result of arms&#146; length negotiations between GSAM and CoreCommodity.&nbsp;They considered this information in light of the overall management
fee expected to be retained by GSAM. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><I>Conclusion </I></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">In connection with their consideration of <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">the&nbsp;Sub-Advisory&nbsp;Agreement,</FONT> the Trustees gave
weight to various factors, but did not identify any particular factor as controlling their decision. After deliberation and consideration of the information provided, including the factors described above, the Trustees present at the meeting,
including a majority of the Independent Trustees, unanimously concluded, in the exercise of their business judgment, that <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">the&nbsp;sub-advisory&nbsp;fees</FONT> to be paid by GSAM to CoreCommodity were reasonable in
light of the factors considered, and that <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">the&nbsp;Sub-Advisory&nbsp;Agreement,</FONT> and the terms thereof, should be approved for a period of two years from its effective date. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Information about CoreCommodity: </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">CoreCommodity Management, LLC, located at 680 Washington Blvd 11th floor, Stamford, CT 06901, is an investment adviser registered with the SEC
and a Commodity Pool Operator and Commodity Trading Advisor registered with the Commodity Futures Trading Commission (CFTC) and a member of the National Futures Association (NFA). The firm had approximately $3.2&nbsp;billion in assets under
management as of June&nbsp;30, 2020. CoreCommodity is wholly-owned by CoreCommodity Capital, LLC, which is controlled by CoreCommodity&#146;s senior management. LAM Holding LLC, a subsidiary of Jefferies Financial Group Inc., has a <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-voting</FONT> interest. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The principal executive officers, directors and managing member of CoreCommodity,
as of the date of this document, are set forth below. The business address of each person is 680 Washington Blvd 11th floor, Stamford, CT 06901. </P> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">CoreCommodity does not act as an investment adviser or
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">sub-adviser</FONT> to any other registered investment company with investment objectives and strategies substantially similar to the Commodity Strategy Fund. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Additional Information About GSAM and the Fund&#146;s Other Service Providers: </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">GSAM, a Delaware limited partnership registered with the SEC as an investment adviser under the Investment Advisers Act of 1940 is the
Fund&#146;s investment adviser. GSAM is an indirect, wholly-owned subsidiary of The Goldman Sachs Group, Inc., a public company that is a bank holding company, financial holding company and a world-wide, full-service financial services organization.
GSAM Holdings LLC is the general partner and principal owner of GSAM. GSAM&#146;s and The Goldman Sachs Group Inc.&#146;s current business address is 200 West Street, New York, NY 10282. As of March&nbsp;31, 2020, GSAM, including its investment
advisory affiliates, had approximately $1.66 trillion in assets under supervision. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Goldman Sachs&nbsp;&amp; Co. LLC, an affiliate of
GSAM, located at 200 West Street, New York, New York 10282, serves as the exclusive distributor of shares of the Fund. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">JPMorgan Chase
Bank, N.A., located at 270 Park Avenue, New York, New York 10017, serves as the Fund&#146;s custodian and administrator. </P>  <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>THE
TRUSTEES UNANIMOUSLY RECOMMEND THAT YOU VOTE IN FAVOR OF PROPOSAL 1. </B></P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P>  <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">12 </P>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B><A NAME="toc_def93780_3"></A>PROPOSAL 2 </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>TO APPROVE THE USE OF A &#147;MANAGER OF MANAGERS&#148; STRUCTURE WHEREBY THE BOARD OF TRUSTEES AND THE INVESTMENT ADVISER WOULD BE
AUTHORIZED TO HIRE AND REPLACE INVESTMENT <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">SUB-ADVISERS</FONT> ON BEHALF OF THE FUND WITHOUT SHAREHOLDER APPROVAL </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Introduction: </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Shareholders of the
Goldman Sachs Commodity Strategy Fund (the &#147;Commodity Strategy Fund&#148; or &#147;Fund&#148;) are being asked to approve a &#147;manager of managers&#148; structure that would permit Goldman Sachs Asset Management, L.P. (the &#147;Investment
Adviser&#148; or &#147;GSAM&#148;) to enter into, or materially amend, <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">sub-advisory</FONT> agreements with any <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">sub-adviser</FONT> retained by GSAM to manage the Fund, upon the
approval of the Board of Trustees and without obtaining Shareholder approval (the &#147;Manager of Managers Structure&#148;). Under the Manager of Managers Structure, GSAM would have the ultimate responsibility, subject to oversight by the Board of
Trustees, to oversee any <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">sub-advisers</FONT> and recommend their hiring, termination and replacement. From the perspective of Shareholders, the role of a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">sub-adviser</FONT> would be
substantially equivalent to the role of individual portfolio managers employed by GSAM. </P>  <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">At a meeting held on July&nbsp;23, 2020, the
Trustees present at the meeting, including those Trustees of the Trust who are not &#147;interested persons,&#148; as defined in the Investment Company Act of 1940 (the &#147;1940 Act&#148;) (the &#147;Independent Trustees&#148;), unanimously
approved the use of the Manager of Managers Structure for the Fund. Although one Trustee was unable to attend this meeting, that Trustee supported the Proposal. The Manager of Managers Structure would be subject to Board oversight and conditions
imposed by the U.S. Securities and Exchange Commission (&#147;SEC&#148;) in an exemptive order. These conditions include a requirement that any <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">sub-advisory</FONT> agreement or material change to such agreement be
approved by the Board, including the Independent Trustees. Information on the exemptive order is described under &#147;The Exemptive Order&#148; below. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Subject to the supervision and approval of the Board and approval of the Shareholders of the Fund, GSAM is responsible for managing the assets
of the Fund and is permitted under the terms of the investment advisory contract with the Fund to engage <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">sub-advisers</FONT> to provide portfolio management services to the Fund. If GSAM delegates <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">sub-advisory</FONT> duties to a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">sub-adviser,</FONT> it remains responsible for monitoring and evaluating the performance of the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">sub-adviser.</FONT> </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The 1940 Act generally requires that a written <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">sub-advisory</FONT> agreement be approved by the affirmative
vote of a majority of the outstanding shares of the Fund. The appointment of a new <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">sub-adviser</FONT> or material modification of an existing <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">sub-advisory</FONT> agreement also must
also be presented for approval by the Fund&#146;s Shareholders as required by the 1940 Act. GSAM and the Board believe that it is in the best interests of Shareholders to provide GSAM and the Board with increased flexibility to recommend, supervise,
evaluate, and change <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">sub-advisers</FONT> without incurring the significant delay and expense associated with obtaining prior Shareholder approval. See &#147;Benefits of a &#145;Manager of Managers&#146;
Structure&#148; below. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>The Exemptive Order: </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The SEC issued an exemptive order (the &#147;Order&#148;) on May&nbsp;30, 2013 permitting GSAM to enter into a new <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">sub-advisory</FONT> agreement or materially amend an existing <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">sub-advisory</FONT> agreement, subject to approval by the Board (including a majority of Independent Trustees), without first
obtaining Shareholder approval. The Order provides that GSAM will compensate the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">sub-adviser</FONT> out of its own assets. The Manager of Managers Structure has previously been implemented by other funds in the GSAM
family of funds. GSAM and the Fund can operate the Fund as a manager of managers fund in reliance upon the Order only if, among other things, the Shareholders of the Fund have approved the Manager of Managers Structure. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P>  <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">13 </P>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Under the terms of the Order, the Fund and GSAM are, and would continue to be, subject to several
conditions imposed by the SEC. For instance, as requested in this Proposal, Shareholder approval is required before GSAM and the Fund may implement the Manager of Managers Structure for the Fund. In addition, the Fund must continue to obtain
Shareholder approval to approve or materially modify a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">sub-advisory</FONT> agreement with an affiliated <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Sub-Adviser</FONT> (as defined below). Further, under the conditions of the
Order, within ninety (90)&nbsp;days of a change to a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">sub-advisory</FONT> arrangement the Fund&#146;s Shareholders must be provided with an information statement that contains information about the <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">sub-adviser</FONT> and <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">sub-advisory</FONT> agreement that would be contained in a proxy statement. The Order also provides that a majority of the Fund&#146;s Board of Trustees consist of
Independent Trustees and the nomination of new or additional Independent Trustees must be at the discretion of the then-existing Independent Trustees. Any changes to a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">sub-advisory</FONT> agreement that would result
in an increase in the overall management and advisory fees of the Fund will be required to be approved by the Shareholders of the Fund. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">If approved by Shareholders, the Manager of Managers Structure will become effective on the same date as the
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Sub-Advisory</FONT> Agreement with CoreCommodity. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Benefits of a Manager of Managers Structure: </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">A Manager of Managers Structure may benefit Shareholders in that it will allow GSAM the additional flexibility to implement <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">sub-adviser</FONT> changes or materially modify <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">sub-advisory</FONT> agreements when needed, and to avoid numerous and expensive proxy solicitations. Such an arrangement may also allow the
Fund to operate with greater efficiency by allowing GSAM to employ <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">sub-advisers</FONT> best suited to the needs of the Fund, without incurring the expense and delays associated with obtaining Shareholder approval. If
the Shareholders approve the Manager of Managers Structure for the Fund, the Fund will continue to obtain Shareholder approval of a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">sub-advisory</FONT> agreement with a
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">sub-adviser</FONT> considered to be an &#147;affiliated person&#148;, as defined in the 1940 Act, of the Fund or GSAM, other than by reason of serving as a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">sub-adviser</FONT> to the
Fund (&#147;affiliated <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Sub-Adviser&#148;).</FONT> </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Currently, to appoint a
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">sub-adviser</FONT> to the Fund or to materially amend a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">sub-advisory</FONT> agreement, the Trust must call and hold a Shareholder meeting of the Fund, create and distribute proxy
materials, and solicit proxy votes from the Fund&#146;s Shareholders. In addition, if a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">sub-adviser</FONT> to the Fund is acquired or there is a change of control of the
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">sub-adviser</FONT> that results in the &#147;assignment&#148; of the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">sub-advisory</FONT> agreement with GSAM, the Trust currently must seek approval of a new <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">sub-advisory</FONT> agreement from Shareholders of the Fund, even when there will be no change in the persons managing the Fund. This process is time-consuming and costly, and some of the costs may be borne by the Fund.
Without the delay inherent in holding a Shareholder meeting, GSAM and the Fund would be able to act more quickly to appoint a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">sub-adviser</FONT> with less expense when the Board and GSAM believe that the appointment
would benefit the Fund. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">If Shareholders of the Fund do not approve the Manager of Managers Structure for the Fund, it will not be
implemented and the Fund will continue to be required to obtain shareholder approval of any changes in the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">sub-adviser</FONT> of the Fund or any material changes to
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">sub-advisory</FONT> agreements. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Evaluation by the Board of Trustees: </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">In determining whether or not it was appropriate to approve the proposed Manager of Managers Structure and to recommend approval of such
arrangement to the Shareholders, the Board, including the Independent Trustees, considered certain information and representations provided by GSAM. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">After carefully considering the Fund&#146;s contractual arrangement under which the Investment Adviser has been engaged as an investment
adviser, and GSAM&#146;s experience in recommending and monitoring <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">sub-advisers,</FONT> the Board believes that it is appropriate to allow the recommendation, supervision and evaluation of <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">sub-advisers</FONT> to be conducted by GSAM. The Board also believes that this approach would be consistent with Shareholders&#146; expectations that GSAM will use its expertise to recommend to the Board qualified
candidates to serve as <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">sub-advisers.</FONT> </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P>  <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">14 </P>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The Board will continue to provide oversight of the
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">sub-adviser</FONT> selection and engagement process. The Board, including a majority of the Independent Trustees, will continue to evaluate and consider for approval all new or amended
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">sub-advisory</FONT> agreements. In addition, under the 1940 Act and the terms of the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">sub-advisory</FONT> agreements, after the initial term the Board, including a majority of the
Independent Trustees, are required to review annually and consider for renewal the agreement. Upon entering into, renewing or amending a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">sub-advisory</FONT> agreement, GSAM and the
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">sub-adviser</FONT> have a legal duty to provide to the Board information on pertinent factors. </P>  <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>THE
TRUSTEES UNANIMOUSLY RECOMMEND THAT YOU VOTE IN FAVOR OF PROPOSAL 2. </B></P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P>  <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">15 </P>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B><A NAME="toc_def93780_4"></A>PROPOSAL 3 </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>TO TRANSACT SUCH OTHER BUSINESS AS MAY PROPERLY COME BEFORE THE MEETING OR ANY POSTPONEMENT OR ADJOURNMENT THEREOF </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The management of the Trust does not know of any other matters to be brought before the Meeting. If such matters are properly brought before the Meeting,
proxies that do not contain specific instructions to the contrary will be voted in accordance with the judgment of the person or persons acting thereunder. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P>  <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">16 </P>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B><A NAME="toc_def93780_5"></A>VOTE REQUIRED FOR APPROVAL OF MATTERS AT THE MEETING </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">A quorum for the transaction of business at the Meeting is established by the presence, in person or by proxy, of holders representing <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">one-third</FONT> of the votes entitled to be cast at the Meeting, but any lesser number will be sufficient for adjournments. Cumulative voting is not permitted. The Proposals will be voted upon by Shareholders of the
Commodity Strategy Fund. The adoption of each Proposal requires an affirmative vote of the lesser of: (i) 67% or more of the voting securities of the Fund that are present at the meeting or represented by proxy, if holders of shares representing
more than 50% of the outstanding voting securities of the Fund are present or represented by proxy; or (ii)&nbsp;more than 50% of the outstanding voting securities of the Fund (a &#147;1940 Act Majority&#148;). </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">If a proxy card is properly executed and returned accompanied by instructions to withhold authority (an abstention), the shares represented
thereby will be counted as shares present and entitled to vote for purposes of determining whether a quorum is present, but will not be counted as a vote in favor of Proposal 1 or 2. Accordingly, abstentions effectively will be a vote against each
Proposal, for which the required vote is a 1940 Act Majority. Ordinarily, <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">broker&nbsp;non-votes,&nbsp;if</FONT> any, would be counted as shares present and entitled to vote for purposes of determining whether a
quorum is present, but would not be counted as a vote in favor of any Proposal. However, because each Proposal is considered <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-routine,</FONT> broker <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-votes</FONT> are
inapplicable to this solicitation and will have no impact on establishing quorum or the votes cast for or against any Proposal.<B> </B> </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">In the event that at the time any session of the Meeting is called to order a quorum is not present in person or by proxy, or if a quorum is
present but sufficient votes in favor of a Proposal have not been received, the Meeting may be adjourned to a later date by the chair of the Meeting or by a vote of Shareholders to permit further solicitation of proxies with respect to a
Proposal.&nbsp;In the event of a Shareholder vote on adjournment, any such adjournment will require the affirmative vote of a majority of the votes cast, and the persons named as proxies will vote those proxies which they are entitled to vote in
favor of any such Proposal in favor of such an adjournment, and will vote those proxies required to be voted against any such Proposal against any such adjournment. The chair of the Meeting may adjourn the Meeting whether or not a quorum is
present.&nbsp;A Shareholder vote may be taken on a Proposal in this Proxy Statement prior to such adjournment if sufficient votes for its approval have been received. Such vote will be considered final regardless of whether the Meeting is adjourned
to permit additional solicitation with respect to any other Proposal. Subject to the foregoing, the Meeting may be adjourned and <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">re-adjourned</FONT> without further notice to Shareholders. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:24pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B><A NAME="toc_def93780_6"></A>SHAREHOLDER PROPOSALS </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The Trust is not required and does not intend to hold a meeting of Shareholders each year. Instead, meetings will be held only when and if
required by law or as otherwise determined by the Board. Any Shareholder desiring to present a proposal for consideration at the next meeting of Shareholders of the Fund must submit the proposal in writing, so that it is received by the Fund within
a reasonable time before any meeting. The proposals should be sent to the Trust at its address stated on the first page of this Proxy Statement. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:24pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B><A NAME="toc_def93780_7"></A>ADDITIONAL INFORMATION </B></P>

Management, L.P. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">200 West Street </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">New York, New York 10282
</P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P>  <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">17 </P>

on the proxy card and follow the instructions on the proxy card. If you have any questions regarding the proxy materials please contact Broadridge at <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">800-574-5796.</FONT></FONT>

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B><A NAME="toc_def93780_8"></A>EXHIBIT A </B></P>
