 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">A-1 </P>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B><A NAME="toc_def93780_9"></A>EXHIBIT B </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>FIVE PERCENT SHAREHOLDERS </B></P>

<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B><A NAME="toc_def93780_10"></A>EXHIBIT C </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>FORM OF <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">SUB-ADVISORY</FONT> AGREEMENT </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">SUB-ADVISORY</FONT> AGREEMENT </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">BETWEEN </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">GOLDMAN SACHS ASSET
MANAGEMENT, L.P. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">and </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">CORECOMMODITY MANAGEMENT, LLC </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><U>GOLDMAN SACHS TRUST </U></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">THIS <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">SUB-ADVISORY</FONT> AGREEMENT (&#147;<U>Agreement</U>&#148;) is made as of [&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;] (the &#147;<U>Effective Date</U>&#148;) by and between <B>GOLDMAN SACHS ASSET MANAGEMENT, L.P.
</B>(&#147;<U>Investment Manager</U>&#148;) and <B>CORECOMMODITY MANAGEMENT, LLC </B>(&#147;<U><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Sub-Adviser</FONT></U>&#148;). </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">WHEREAS, Goldman Sachs Trust, a Delaware statutory trust (&#147;<U>Trust</U>&#148;), is registered as an
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">open-end</FONT> management investment company under the Investment Company Act of 1940, as amended (&#147;<U>1940 Act</U>&#148;) and has elected to be a regulated investment company under Subchapter M of the Internal
Revenue Code; and </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">WHEREAS, pursuant to a Management Agreement (&#147;<U>Management Agreement</U>&#148;) by and between the Trust and the
Investment Manager, a copy of which has been provided to the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Sub-Adviser,</FONT> the Trust has appointed the Investment Manager to furnish investment advisory and other services to the Trust on behalf of the series
of the Trust; and </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">WHEREAS, the Management Agreement authorizes the Investment Manager to provide, either directly or through third
parties, investment advisory services with respect to each series of the Trust; and </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">WHEREAS, subject to the terms and provisions of this
Agreement, the Investment Manager desires to retain the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Sub-Adviser</FONT> to furnish <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">sub-investment</FONT> advisory services on behalf of the series of the Trust listed on Annex A,
as such Annex A may be amended from time to time (such series being collectively referred to herein as the &#147;<U>Fund</U>,&#148; with any reference herein to the Fund pertaining to such series of the Trust as the context requires); </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">NOW, THEREFORE, in consideration of the promises and mutual covenants herein contained, it is agreed between the parties hereto as follows:
</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>1. </B><B><U>Engagement of the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Sub-Adviser</FONT></U></B>. (a)&nbsp;The Investment Manager hereby
engages the services of the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Sub-Adviser</FONT> in furtherance of the Management Agreement with the Trust on behalf of the Fund. The Investment Manager may, in its sole discretion, allocate all, only a portion or none
of the Fund&#146;s assets to the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Sub-Adviser</FONT> for management. The <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Sub-Adviser</FONT> will be responsible for the investment of only the assets which the Investment Manager
allocates to the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Sub-Adviser</FONT> for management under this Agreement, plus all investments, reinvestments and proceeds of the sale thereof, including, without limitation, all interest, dividends and appreciation
on investments, less depreciation thereof and withdrawals by the Investment Manager therefrom (the &#147;<U>Allocated Assets</U>&#148;), there being no minimum or maximum percentage of the Fund&#146;s assets to be allocated to the <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Sub-Adviser</FONT> from time to time hereunder. The <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Sub-Adviser</FONT> accepts its engagement under this Section&nbsp;1. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(b) Pursuant to this Agreement and subject to the supervision and oversight of the Investment Manager, the
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Sub-Adviser</FONT> shall, with respect to the Allocated Assets, provide the Fund with investment research, advice and supervision and furnish a continuous investment program for and manage the investment and
reinvestment of the Allocated Assets. In this regard, the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Sub-Adviser</FONT> shall, with respect to the Allocated Assets, determine in its discretion the securities, cash and other financial instruments to be
purchased, retained or sold for the Fund within the parameters of the investment approach, policies, restrictions and guidelines applicable to the Allocated </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">C-1 </P>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">
Assets as provided by the Investment Manager to the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Sub-Adviser,</FONT> as amended in writing from time to time by the Investment Manager (the &#147;<U>Investment
Guidelines</U>&#148;), the provisions of this Agreement, all applicable laws, rules and regulations and the Fund&#146;s registration statement on Form <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">N-1A</FONT> under the 1940 Act as amended from time to time, or
any successor form thereto (the &#147;<U>Registration Statement</U>&#148;), provided that, notwithstanding any other provision of this Agreement, the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Sub-Adviser</FONT> shall not be responsible for compliance with,
or held liable for failure to take any action in accordance with, the Investment Guidelines, the Registration Statement, any policies, procedures, Counterparty Terms (as defined below) applicable to the Fund or any instructions regarding the Fund,
the Board/Investment Manager Procedures (as defined below) or any supplements or amendments to any of the foregoing, unless and until the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Sub-Adviser</FONT> has received such materials (or has been notified of the
public availability of such materials) in writing. The <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Sub-Adviser</FONT> shall not invest any of the Allocated Assets in any investment that the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Sub-Adviser</FONT> knows or
reasonably should know based on the terms of the constituent documents of the investment, or language in the offering memorandum, prospectus or other offering material, may not be purchased or held by <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">open-end</FONT>
management investment companies registered under the 1940 Act or regulated investment companies under Subchapter M of the Internal Revenue Code, unless such investment may be made after meeting applicable conditions (such as obtaining a waiver) and
the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Sub-Adviser</FONT> has first notified the Investment Manager to discuss an appropriate course of action. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(c) The <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Sub-Adviser&#146;s</FONT> authority hereunder shall include the power to buy, sell, and hold such
securities, cash and other instruments, to open accounts and execute, as agent of the Investment Manager and/or the Trust on behalf of the Fund, trading agreements and any other reasonable and customary documents, representation letters, releases,
consents, elections and confirmations, and any schedules and annexes to any of the foregoing, on behalf of the Fund with respect to the Allocated Assets as the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Sub-Adviser</FONT> deems appropriate within the
parameters of Section&nbsp;1(b) and the conditions of this Agreement. The <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Sub-Adviser</FONT> agrees that, prior to (i)&nbsp;opening (or amending) any accounts, including prime brokerage and futures clearing accounts
with brokerage firms or other financial institutions on behalf of the Fund and (ii)&nbsp;entering into (or amending) any ISDA master agreement, master repurchase agreement, or any other master swap or <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">over-the-counter</FONT></FONT> trading documentation, including any schedule or credit support annex thereto (such agreements collectively, &#147;OTC Agreements&#148;), or any related clearing agreements or control
agreements on behalf of the Fund, the Fund shall have an opportunity to review and consent to the terms of, and the use of, any such account opening documents, prime brokerage, futures and other related agreements, OTC Agreements, and related
clearing agreements or control agreements. The exercise or the performance of any consent right by the Fund (as described above) shall not relieve the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Sub-Adviser</FONT> of its liability, if any, or responsibilities
hereunder. With respect to transactions involving derivative instruments and/or OTC Agreements, the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Sub-Adviser</FONT> agrees to comply with &#147;Counterparty Terms&#148; as provided by the Investment Manager to the
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Sub-Adviser</FONT> in writing from time to time with respect to each applicable Counterparty (as defined below) and each applicable transaction with a Counterparty and to provide Counterparty reports of the type
described in Section&nbsp;6(c). For purposes of this section, the term &#147;Counterparty&#148; includes a clearing broker, prime broker, dealer, foreign currency dealer, futures commission merchant, bank, or any counterparty to an OTC Agreement.
</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(d) The <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Sub-Adviser</FONT> is hereby appointed the Fund&#146;s agent and
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">attorney-in-fact</FONT></FONT> to exercise in its discretion all rights and perform all duties which may be exercisable in relation to any Allocated Assets, including without
limitation the right to vote (or in its discretion, refrain from voting), tender, exchange, endorse, transfer, or deliver any securities on behalf of the Fund, distribution, plan of reorganization, creditors committee, merger, combination,
consolidation, liquidation, underwriting, or similar plan with reference to such securities; and to execute and bind the Fund in waivers, consents and covenants related thereto. For the avoidance of doubt, the
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Sub-Adviser</FONT> has sole and full discretion to vote (or not to vote) any securities in the Allocated Assets and neither the Fund nor the Investment Manager will, directly or indirectly, attempt to influence the <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Sub-Adviser&#146;s</FONT> voting decisions. Further, to the extent the Investment Manager is affiliated with a bank holding company, the Investment Manager will not provide instruction to the
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Sub-Adviser</FONT> on how to vote securities of any U.S. bank holding company (as that term is defined in the Bank Holding Company Act of 1956, as amended). The <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Sub-Adviser</FONT>
represents and covenants that it has adopted written proxy voting policies and procedures as required under Rule <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">206(4)-6</FONT> of the Investment Advisers Act of 1940, as amended (&#147;<U>Advisers Act</U>&#148;), a
copy of </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">C-2 </P>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">
which has been provided to the Fund and the Trust&#146;s Board of Trustees (the &#147;<U>Board</U>&#148;), and that it will promptly provide, with respect to any period in which the <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Sub-Adviser</FONT> has or intends to trade equity securities for the Fund (i)&nbsp;annual updates, and any interim material updates, of such policies and procedures to the Fund and the Board, (ii)&nbsp;its voting records
with respect to the Allocated Assets to the Fund&#146;s proxy voting service, identifying such voting records as the voting records of the Fund, to enable the Fund to meet its annual disclosure requirement pursuant to Rule <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">30b1-4</FONT> under the 1940 Act, and (iii)&nbsp;upon written request therefor, reports to the Investment Manager and/or the Board, as the Fund may direct, in instances where the
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Sub-Adviser</FONT> votes counter to its proxy voting policies. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(e) The
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Sub-Adviser</FONT> shall discharge its responsibilities hereunder subject to the supervision of the Investment Manager, the Board and the officers of the Trust and in compliance with (i)&nbsp;the 1940 Act and the
Advisers Act, and the rules and regulations adopted under each from time to time; (ii)&nbsp;the requirements of Subchapter M of the Internal Revenue Code of 1986, as amended (the &#147;<U>Internal Revenue Code</U>&#148;) applicable to regulated
investment companies (as defined in the Internal Revenue Code); (iii) the Commodity Exchange Act, as amended (&#147;<U>CEA</U>&#148;), and the rules and regulations adopted thereunder from time to time; (iv)&nbsp;all other applicable federal, state
and foreign laws and regulations, including without limitation, the rules of any self-regulatory organization; (v)&nbsp;the Trust&#146;s Amended and Restated Declaration of Trust and <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">By-Laws,</FONT> as each may be
amended from time to time; (vi)&nbsp;the objectives, policies and limitations for the Fund set forth in the Registration Statement (to the extent applicable to the Allocated Assets); and (vii)&nbsp;the Investment Guidelines and such other
guidelines, policies and procedures adopted by the Board or implemented by the Investment Manager with respect to the Fund or to the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Sub-Adviser&#146;s</FONT> activities under this Agreement and, in all cases,
provided to the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Sub-Adviser</FONT> in writing from time to time (&#147;<U>Board/Investment Manager Procedures</U>&#148;). For avoidance of doubt, with respect to the
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Sub-Adviser&#146;s</FONT> compliance with the foregoing requirements as they pertain to the Allocated Assets, the Investment Manager agrees that the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Sub-Adviser</FONT> shall be
entitled to treat the Allocated Assets as constituting the entire portfolio of a registered investment company or regulated investment company, as the context requires. The <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Sub-Adviser</FONT> shall maintain
compliance procedures and/or operational processes for the Allocated Assets reasonably designed to prevent violations of the foregoing, as applicable, and that the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Sub-Adviser</FONT> reasonably believes are adequate
to prevent violations of applicable law. No supervisory activity undertaken by the Investment Manager shall limit the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Sub-Adviser&#146;s</FONT> full responsibility for any of the foregoing. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(f) The <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Sub-Adviser</FONT> shall not consult with any other
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">sub-investment</FONT> adviser for the Fund or the Trust or any other fund under common control with the Trust, concerning transactions for the Fund in securities or other assets, except that such consultations are
permitted between the current and successor <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">sub-investment</FONT> advisers of the Fund in order to effect an orderly transition of <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">sub-advisory</FONT> duties so long as such
consultations are not concerning transactions prohibited by Section&nbsp;17(a) of the 1940 Act. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(g) In providing investment advisory
services to the Fund pursuant to this Agreement, the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Sub-Adviser</FONT> shall not provide any such services from any jurisdiction other than the United States of America or any other jurisdiction that the Investment
Manager may permit in writing (each of the foregoing, an &#147;<U>Authorized Jurisdiction</U>&#148;). In the event that the Investment Manager notifies the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Sub-Adviser</FONT> in writing that it is no longer permitted
to provide services to the Fund from an Authorized Jurisdiction, such jurisdiction shall cease to be an Authorized Jurisdiction and the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Sub-Adviser</FONT> shall promptly cease providing services to the Fund from such
jurisdiction. With respect to any services provided by the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Sub-Adviser</FONT> from an Authorized Jurisdiction, the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Sub-Adviser</FONT> shall ensure that none of its portfolio managers,
traders or other employees, agents or representatives conduct their activities on behalf of the Fund in a manner that would create in such jurisdiction a permanent establishment or other taxable presence for the Fund or its investors. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>2. </B><B><U>Fund Transactions</U></B>. (a)&nbsp;In connection with purchases and sales of securities and other instruments for the
Allocated Assets, neither the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Sub-Adviser</FONT> nor its affiliated persons (as defined in the 1940 Act) or any of their respective partners, officers or employees shall act as principal, except as otherwise
permitted by the 1940 Act. In no instance will securities be purchased from or sold to the Investment Manager or any of its affiliated persons, except in accordance with the 1940 Act, the Advisers Act, and the rules under each, and all other
</P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">C-3 </P>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">
federal, state and foreign laws or regulations applicable to the Fund. Unless specifically permitted by the 1940 Act (and the rules thereunder) or Board/Investment Manager Procedures, the <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Sub-Adviser</FONT> agrees that it will not execute any portfolio transactions for the Allocated Assets with a broker or dealer which is (i)&nbsp;an affiliated person of the Fund, including the Investment Manager; or
(ii)&nbsp;an affiliated person of such an affiliated person, provided that the Investment Manager has previously provided a list of such brokers and/or dealers to the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Sub-Adviser</FONT> and will periodically provide
any updates to such list to the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Sub-Adviser.</FONT> The Investment Manager also agrees that it will provide the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Sub-Adviser</FONT> with a written list (if different from the list
described in the previous sentence) of all affiliated persons of the Fund, all principal underwriters of the Fund&#146;s shares and all affiliated persons of such affiliated persons or principal underwriters (other than affiliated persons of the <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Sub-Adviser)</FONT> and will periodically provide any updates to such list to the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Sub-Adviser.</FONT> The <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Sub-Adviser</FONT> or its agents shall arrange for
the placing of orders for the purchase and sale of portfolio securities and other instruments for the Fund&#146;s account either directly with the issuer or with any broker or dealer, foreign currency dealer, futures commission merchant or other
party selected by the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Sub-Adviser</FONT> (each of the foregoing, a &#147;<U>Transaction Party</U>&#148;), provided that the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Sub-Adviser</FONT> complies with the Counterparty Terms
described in Section&nbsp;1(c) with respect to each such Transaction Party. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(b) In the selection of such brokers or dealers and the
placing of such orders the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Sub-Adviser</FONT> is directed at all times to seek to obtain for the Fund the most favorable execution possible, taking into account such factors as it deems relevant, which may include,
without limitation, breadth of and availability of accurate information regarding the market in the investment, price (including the applicable brokerage commission or dealer spread), size and type of the order, difficulty of execution, the timing
of the transaction taking into account market prices and trends, the reputation, experience, financial condition, execution capability, past execution history and operational facilities of the brokerage firm, the extent to which the brokerage firm
makes a market in the investments involved or has access to such market, the liquidity of the market for the investments, the quality and usefulness of investment ideas presented by the brokerage firm, the brokerage firm&#146;s expertise in the
specific investments or sectors in which the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Sub-Adviser</FONT> seeks to trade, the brokerage firm&#146;s ability to accommodate any special execution or order handling requirements that may surround the particular
transaction, the brokerage firm&#146;s risk and skill in positioning blocks of securities, and confidentiality considerations. It is also understood that it may be desirable for the Fund that the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Sub-Adviser</FONT>
have access to supplemental investment and market research and security and economic analyses that are consistent with Section&nbsp;28(e) of the Securities Exchange Act of 1934, as amended (the &#147;<U>1934 Act</U>&#148;), and are provided by
brokers who may execute brokerage transactions at a higher cost to the Fund than may result when allocating brokerage to other brokers on the basis of seeking the most favorable price and efficient execution. Therefore, subject to compliance with
the safe harbor provided by Section&nbsp;28(e) of the 1934 Act and such other conditions and limitations as may be established by the Investment Manager from time to time, if any, the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Sub-Adviser</FONT> is authorized
to consider such services provided to the Fund and other accounts over which the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Sub-Adviser</FONT> or any of its affiliates exercises investment discretion and to place orders for the purchase and sale of securities
for the Fund with such brokers, if the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Sub-Adviser</FONT> determines in good faith that the amount of commissions for executing such portfolio transactions is reasonable in relation to the value of the brokerage and
research services provided by such brokers, viewed in terms of either that particular transaction or the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Sub-Adviser&#146;s</FONT> overall responsibilities with respect to the Allocated Assets and/or to other clients
of the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Sub-Adviser</FONT> as to which the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Sub-Adviser</FONT> exercises investment discretion, subject to review by the Investment Manager and the Board from time to time with respect
to the extent and continuation of this practice. It is understood that the services provided by such brokers may be useful to the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Sub-Adviser</FONT> in connection with its services to other clients. The <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Sub-Adviser,</FONT> on occasions when it deems the purchase or sale of a security to be in the best interests of the Fund as well as its other clients, may, but shall be under no obligation to, aggregate, to the extent
permitted by applicable laws, rules and regulations, the securities to be sold or purchased in order to obtain the most favorable execution. In such event, allocation of the securities so purchased or sold, as well as the expenses incurred in the
transaction, shall be made by the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Sub-Adviser</FONT> in the manner it considers to be the most equitable over time and consistent with its obligations to the Fund and to such other clients. The Board may from time to
time adopt policies and procedures that modify and/or restrict the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Sub-Adviser&#146;s</FONT> authority regarding the execution of the Fund&#146;s portfolio transactions provided herein. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">C-4 </P>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(c) The <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Sub-Adviser</FONT> shall not acquire on behalf of the
Fund any equity securities registered under Section&nbsp;12 of the 1934 Act with the purpose or effect, at the time of such acquisition, of changing or influencing control of the issuer of the securities or in connection with or as a participant in
any transaction having such purpose or effect, including any transaction subject to Rule <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">13d-3(b)</FONT> promulgated under the 1934 Act. The <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Sub-Adviser</FONT> further agrees that it
will prepare and cause to be filed in a timely manner (i)&nbsp;if required, quarterly information on Form 13F, which shall include all applicable securities within the Allocated Assets (it being understood that the
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Sub-Adviser</FONT> shall consider such securities as being subject to its investment discretion for purposes of Section&nbsp;13(f) of the 1934 Act), and (ii)&nbsp;if required, periodic information on Schedule 13D or
13G, as applicable, reporting such securities as being beneficially owned by the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Sub-Adviser</FONT> for purposes of Rule <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">13d-3</FONT> under the 1934 Act. If any investments made by
the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Sub-Adviser</FONT> on behalf of the Fund are required to be disclosed in such reports or in any other reports to be filed by the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Sub-Adviser</FONT> with any governmental or
self-regulatory agency or organization or exchange in a manner that identifies such investments as being held by or for the benefit of the Fund, the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Sub-Adviser</FONT> shall provide the Investment Manager with prompt
written notice thereof, setting forth in reasonable detail the nature of the report and the investments of the Fund to be reported. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(d)
The <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Sub-Adviser</FONT> hereby agrees not to cause the Fund to engage in any &#147;U.S. Equity Derivative Transaction&#148; (as defined below) where the Fund is the short party to the transaction, unless, at all
relevant times, the long party is either (i)&nbsp;a U.S. broker or dealer or (ii)&nbsp;a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-U.S.</FONT> broker or dealer that is a qualified derivatives dealer. For purposes of this section, a &#147;U.S. Equity
Derivative Transaction&#148; is any securities lending or sale-repurchase transaction, notional principal contract or equity-linked instrument that is described in Treasury Regulations
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Section&nbsp;1.871-15(a)(12),</FONT> IRS Notice <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">2016-76</FONT> or any amended or successor guidance. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>3. </B><B><U>Compensation of the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Sub-Adviser</FONT></U></B>. (a)&nbsp;For all services to be rendered and
payments made as provided in this Agreement, the Investment Manager shall pay the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Sub-Adviser,</FONT> in arrears, each calendar quarter a fee at an annual rate equal to the percentage of the average daily net
Allocated Assets, set forth with respect to the Fund on Annex A. The &#147;average daily net Allocated Assets&#148; shall be determined on the basis set forth in the Fund&#146;s prospectus(es) or otherwise consistent with the 1940 Act and the rules
and regulations thereunder. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(b) The fee for any calendar quarter during which this Agreement is in effect for less than the entire
quarter shall be <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">pro-rated</FONT> based on the number of calendar days during such quarter that the Agreement was in effect. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(c) If, at any time, (i)&nbsp;the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Sub-Adviser</FONT> or any of its affiliated persons provides as a
subadviser to any other investment company registered under the 1940 Act investment advisory services using substantially similar strategies to those provided by the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Sub-Adviser</FONT> to the Fund pursuant to this
Agreement, (ii)&nbsp;the value of the assets under management with respect to which the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Sub-Adviser</FONT> provides such services to such other investment company is the same as or less than the value of the
Allocated Assets, and (iii)&nbsp;the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Sub-Adviser</FONT> is compensated for providing such services at a rate less than the rate set forth on Annex A, then the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Sub-Adviser</FONT> shall
promptly notify the Investment Manager of the foregoing in reasonable detail and, as of the date of such notice, the rate set forth on Annex A shall immediately and without requirement of further action be deemed amended to reflect a rate equal to
the lower rate at which the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Sub-Adviser</FONT> is compensated by such other investment company. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>4.
</B><B><U>Expenses</U></B>. The <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Sub-Adviser</FONT> agrees, at its own expense, to render the services set forth herein and to provide the office space, furnishings, equipment and personnel required by it to perform
such services on the terms and for the compensation provided in this Agreement. The Fund shall be responsible for payment of brokerage commissions, transfer fees, registration costs, clearing and custody fees, transaction-related taxes and other
similar costs and transaction-related expenses and fees arising out of transactions effected on behalf of the Fund, which shall be deducted from the Allocated Assets. Subject to the foregoing, the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Sub-Adviser</FONT>
will pay all expenses incurred by it in connection with its activities under this Agreement, including without limitation, all costs associated with attending or otherwise participating in regular or special meetings of the Board or shareholders, or
with the Investment Manager, as requested, and additions or modifications to the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Sub-Adviser&#146;s</FONT> operations necessary to perform its services hereunder in compliance with this Agreement, the Investment
Guidelines, any other Board/Investment Manager Procedures and applicable law. The <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Sub-Adviser</FONT> shall be </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">C-5 </P>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">
responsible for all costs associated with any information statements and/or other disclosure materials that are for the sole benefit of, and occur as a direct result of any event occurring with
respect to, the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Sub-Adviser</FONT> (including, but not limited to, the legal fees associated with preparation, printing, filing and mailing thereof, as well as any shareholder meeting and/or solicitation costs, if
applicable). </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>5.</B><B></B><B><U>&nbsp;Delivery of Information, Reports and Certain Notifications</U></B>. (a)&nbsp;The Investment
Manager shall cause the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Sub-Adviser</FONT> to be kept informed with regard to the funds available, or to become available, for investment. Without limiting the foregoing, the Investment Manager shall provide, or
shall cause to be provided, to the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Sub-Adviser</FONT> on a daily basis such timely information relating to the Fund&#146;s capital activity as the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Sub-Adviser</FONT> reasonably
requests. The Investment Manager agrees to furnish to the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Sub-Adviser</FONT> current prospectuses, statements of additional information, proxy statements, reports to shareholders, financial statements, Amended and
Restated Declaration of Trust and <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">By-Laws</FONT> and such other information with regard to the affairs of the Fund as the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Sub-Adviser</FONT> may reasonably request. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(b) The <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Sub-Adviser</FONT> shall report regularly on a timely basis to the Investment Manager and to the
Board and shall make appropriate persons, including portfolio managers, available for the purpose of reviewing with representatives of the Investment Manager and the Board on a regular basis at reasonable times the management of the Allocated
Assets, the performance of the Allocated Assets in relation to standard industry indices and the Fund&#146;s own performance benchmark, and general conditions affecting the marketplace. The <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Sub-Adviser</FONT> agrees
to render to the Investment Manager and the Board on a timely basis such other periodic and special reports regarding its activities under this Agreement as the Investment Manager or the Board may reasonably request. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(c) The <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Sub-Adviser</FONT> shall provide the Investment Manager, the Fund or the Board with such information
and assurances (including certifications and <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">sub-certifications)</FONT> and with such assistance as the Investment Manager, the Fund or the Board may reasonably request from time to time in order to assist it in
complying with applicable laws, rules, regulations and exemptive orders, including requirements in connection with the Investment Manager&#146;s, the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Sub-Adviser&#146;s</FONT> or the Board&#146;s fulfillment of its
responsibilities under Section&nbsp;15(c) of the 1940 Act and the preparation and/or filing of periodic and other reports and filings required to maintain the registration and qualification of the Fund, or to meet other regulatory or tax
requirements applicable to the Fund, under federal and state, and foreign securities, commodities and tax laws and other applicable laws. The <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Sub-Adviser</FONT> shall review such portions of draft reports to
shareholders, registration statements or amendments thereto and other documents that relate to the Allocated Assets or the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Sub-Adviser</FONT> provided to the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Sub-Adviser</FONT> with
reasonable advance notice to the extent practicable under the circumstances, provide comments on such drafts on a timely basis, and provide certifications or <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">sub-certifications</FONT> on a timely basis as to the
accuracy of the information provided by the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Sub-Adviser</FONT> and/or contained in such reports or other documents that relates to the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Sub-Adviser</FONT> or the Allocated Assets. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(d) The <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Sub-Adviser</FONT> agrees to provide and update no less frequently than quarterly a list of all the
affiliated persons of the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Sub-Adviser,</FONT> provided that the Investment Manager will request such update quarterly in connection with the quarterly compliance process identified in Section&nbsp;6(f) below, and the
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Sub-Adviser&#146;s</FONT> confirmation that no new affiliates have been added or removed during the applicable quarter will suffice for the update required under this Section&nbsp;5(d). </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(e) If required by the CEA or the rules and regulations thereunder promulgated by the Commodity Futures Trading Commission
(&#147;<U>CFTC</U>&#148;), the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Sub-Adviser</FONT> will provide the Fund with a copy of its most recent CFTC disclosure document or a written explanation of the reason why it is not required to deliver such a
disclosure document. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>6.</B><B></B><B><U>&nbsp;Cooperation with the Fund, the Investment Manager and Other Service Providers</U></B>.
(a)&nbsp;The <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Sub-Adviser</FONT> agrees to cooperate with and provide reasonable assistance to the Investment Manager, the Fund, the Fund&#146;s custodian, accounting agent, administrator, pricing agents, independent
auditors and all other agents, representatives and service providers of the Fund and the Investment Manager, and to provide the foregoing persons such information with respect to the Allocated Assets as they may reasonably request from time to time
</P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">C-6 </P>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">
in the performance of their obligations; provide prompt responses to reasonable requests made by such persons; and establish and maintain appropriate operational programs, procedures and
interfaces with such persons so as to promote the efficient exchange of information and compliance with applicable laws, rules and regulations, and the guidelines, policies and procedures adopted or implemented with respect to the Fund and/or the <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Sub-Adviser.</FONT> </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(b) The Fund&#146;s assets (including the Allocated Assets) shall be held by a custodian
appointed by the Fund pursuant to a separate custody agreement; the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Sub-Adviser</FONT> and its affiliates shall at no time have custody or physical control of any assets or cash of the Fund. The <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Sub-Adviser</FONT> shall have the authority to instruct the Fund&#146;s custodian: (i)&nbsp;to pay cash for securities and other property delivered to the custodian, (ii)&nbsp;to deliver securities and other property
against payment for the Allocated Assets, (iii)&nbsp;to allocate assets between the Fund and the Subsidiary under Section&nbsp;1(e) above, and (iv)&nbsp;to transfer assets and funds to such accounts as the
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Sub-Adviser</FONT> may designate, all consistent with the powers, authorities and limitations set forth herein. The <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Sub-Adviser</FONT> shall advise the Fund&#146;s custodian and
accounting agent on a prompt basis of each purchase and sale of a portfolio security or other financial instrument specifying the name of the issuer or Counterparty, the description, terms and amount of shares or principal amount of the security or
other financial instrument purchased or sold, the market price, commission and gross or net price, trade date, settlement date and identity of the effecting broker or dealer and such other information as may reasonably be required. The <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Sub-Adviser</FONT> shall arrange for the transmission to the Fund&#146;s custodian and accounting agent on a daily basis such confirmation, trade tickets, and other documents and information as may be reasonably necessary
to enable the custodian and accounting agent to perform their administrative, recordkeeping and other responsibilities with respect to the Fund. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(c) Without limiting the generality of the foregoing and in furtherance thereof, the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Sub-Adviser</FONT> shall
report to the Fund&#146;s custodian and accounting agent all trades and positions among the Allocated Assets daily (in such form and at such times as specified by the Fund&#146;s custodian and accounting agent and/or the Investment Manager),
including any trade it has entered into for which it has not received confirmation (and, with respect to transactions involving derivative instruments, shall also request each executing broker and Counterparty to deliver its own such transaction and
position reporting), and any information related to any corporate action relevant to the investments of the Allocated Assets (in such form and at such times as specified by the Fund&#146;s custodian and accounting agent). Unless otherwise specified
by the Investment Manager, all trades shall be communicated by the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Sub-Adviser</FONT> to the Fund&#146;s custodian and accounting agent by 11 a.m. Eastern Time on the business day following the trade date. The <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Sub-Adviser</FONT> shall notify the Fund&#146;s custodian and accounting agent immediately upon becoming aware of any trades not included in any previously transmitted trade communication. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(d) The <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Sub-Adviser</FONT> shall reconcile all trades and positions with each executing broker and
Counterparty daily to ensure accurate trade settlement and verify open positions (including cash).&nbsp;The <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Sub-Adviser</FONT> shall also reconcile daily all trades and positions (including cash) to the Fund&#146;s
official books and records, including without limitation, daily reconciliation of all open Custody Positions (as defined below) (including cash) to the custodian, and a daily reconciliation of all open Counterparty-Traded Positions (as defined
below) to the accounting agent. The Fund&#146;s accounting agent shall also conduct a reconciliation of Counterparty-Traded Positions (as defined below) as reported from executing brokers and Counterparties and the
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Sub-Adviser</FONT> shall cooperate with the Fund&#146;s accounting agent in order to effect such reconciliation, including without limitation by arranging for access by the Fund&#146;s custodian and accounting agent
to such files and websites of the executing brokers and Counterparties as the Fund&#146;s accounting agent may reasonably request.&nbsp;The <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Sub-Adviser</FONT> shall work with the Fund&#146;s custodian and accounting
agent and/or the Investment Manager, as appropriate, to resolve all open reconciliation items on the same day that they are identified, including trade and position discrepancies, identified in such reconciliations.&nbsp;The <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Sub-Adviser</FONT> shall also provide to the Investment Manager and its custodian and accounting agent a monthly (or such other frequency as may be reasonably requested by the Investment Manager) report detailing all the
reconciliation activities outlined in this section performed during the previous monthly period (or such other period as reasonably requested), including details about each discrepancy and the plan for resolution.&nbsp;These reports shall be sent to
the email addresses as provided by the Investment Manager. If a reconciliation does not identify any discrepancies, an email is still required providing evidence of reconciliation.&nbsp;For purposes of this Section&nbsp;6(d), the term &#147;Custody
Positions&#148; refers to all Allocated Assets of </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">C-7 </P>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">
the Fund, including cash, for which custody is maintained directly by the Fund&#146;s custodian and the term &#147;Counterparty-Traded Positions&#148; refers to all other Allocated Assets of the
Fund, including instruments traded via a Counterparty as defined in Section&nbsp;1(c). </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(e) The
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Sub-Adviser</FONT> shall, upon request, use reasonable efforts to provide assistance to the Board, the Investment Manager, the custodian or administrator for the Fund in determining or confirming, consistent with the
Board/Investment Manager Procedures and the Registration Statement, the value of any portfolio securities or other assets or liabilities of the Allocated Assets for which the Investment Manager, custodian or administrator seeks assistance from the <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Sub-Adviser</FONT> or identifies for review by the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Sub-Adviser.</FONT> This assistance includes (but is not limited to): (i) designating and providing reasonable access to one or more
employees of the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Sub-Adviser</FONT> who are knowledgeable about the security or other asset or liability, its issuer or counterparty (as applicable), its financial condition, trading and/or other relevant factors for
valuation, which employees shall be available for consultation when the Board or a designated committee thereof convenes; (ii)&nbsp;assisting the Board, Investment Manager, the custodian or the administrator in obtaining bids and offers or quotes
from broker-dealers or market-makers with respect to investments held in the Allocated Assets, upon the reasonable request of the Investment Manager, custodian or administrator; (iii)&nbsp;upon the reasonable request of the Board, Investment
Manager, the custodian or the administrator, providing recommendations for pricing and fair valuations (including the methodology and rationale used in making such recommendation and such other relevant information as may be requested); and
(iv)&nbsp;maintaining adequate records and written backup information with respect to the investments valuation assistance provided hereunder, and providing such information to the Board, Investment Manager or the Fund upon reasonable request, with
such records being deemed Fund records. The <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Sub-Adviser</FONT> shall promptly notify the Investment Manager if, for any reason, the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Sub-Adviser</FONT> believes that the price of any
security or other investment among the Allocated Assets may not accurately reflect the value thereof. Additionally, the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Sub-Adviser</FONT> shall use reasonable efforts, upon request of the Investment Manager, to
obtain valuations for derivative instruments from Counterparties and to provide such information, and any other relevant input in relation to valuation determinations suggested by the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Sub-Adviser</FONT> at the
reasonable request of the Investment Manager, to the Fund&#146;s accounting agent and the Investment Manager for their consideration as specified by the Investment Manager. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(f) From time to time as the Board or the Investment Manager may reasonably request, the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Sub-Adviser</FONT>
shall furnish to the Investment Manager, the Board and the officers of the Trust reports on portfolio transactions and reports on issuers of securities and other financial instruments, Counterparties and underlying reference terms of OTC Agreements
and any other relevant information regarding any positions held in the portfolio, all in such detail as the Trust or the Investment Manager may reasonably request, including but not limited to, quarterly reports documenting the <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Sub-Adviser&#146;s</FONT> compliance with Sections 10(f), 17(a) and 17(e) of the 1940 Act, and the rules thereunder, in its management of the Allocated Assets, quarterly compliance checklists developed for the Fund by the
Investment Manager, quarterly certifications under Rule <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">38a-1</FONT> of the 1940 Act and under Rule <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">206(4)-7</FONT> of the Advisers Act, annual reports under Rule <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">206(4)-7</FONT> of the Advisers Act and an annual due diligence questionnaire and, to the extent available, any external third party audit reports, including pursuant to Statement on Standards for Attestation Engagements
(SSAE) No.&nbsp;18. Without limiting the foregoing, the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Sub-Adviser</FONT> agrees that it shall certify to the Fund on a timely basis after the end of each calendar quarter that it has complied with all of the
Investment Guidelines, all applicable laws and regulations and other conditions and agreements contained herein during the prior calendar quarter. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(g) In addition, the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Sub-Adviser</FONT> shall assist the Fund and the Investment Manager in complying with
the provisions of the Sarbanes-Oxley Act of 2002 and shall provide certifications in the form reasonably requested by the Fund relating to the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Sub-Adviser&#146;s</FONT> services under this Agreement. The <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Sub-Adviser</FONT> shall provide necessary support to the Fund and the Investment Manager in preparing and presenting the Fund&#146;s financial statements, and in doing so shall be responsible for applying appropriate
accounting and financial reporting principles and maintaining policies and internal controls and procedures, including internal controls over financial reporting, designed to reasonably assure compliance with generally accepted accounting principles
(GAAP) and applicable laws and regulations. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">C-8 </P>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(h) The <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Sub-Adviser</FONT> shall further notify the Investment
Manager promptly upon detection of any error in connection with its management of the Allocated Assets, including but not limited to any trade errors. In addition, in the event of any such error, the
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Sub-Adviser</FONT> shall also provide a memorandum to the Investment Manager that sufficiently describes any such error and the action to be taken to prevent future occurrences of such error or, alternatively, a
statement that the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Sub-Adviser</FONT> has reviewed the relevant controls, and has determined those controls are reasonably designed to prevent additional errors in the future (and, to the extent relevant, that such
controls are reasonably designed to prevent violations of the federal securities laws), and as such no further action is required. Further, the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Sub-Adviser</FONT> shall provide access to the Investment Manager and
the Fund, or their agents, to all documents and information related to any such error, its analysis and correction, and the correction of all such errors impacting the Fund must be corrected to the satisfaction of the Investment Manager and the
Fund. Notwithstanding Section&nbsp;14, the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Sub-Adviser</FONT> will reimburse the Fund for costs, losses or damages incurred arising out of or resulting from such error, if any; provided, however, that the <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Sub-Adviser</FONT> need not reimburse the Fund for any costs, losses or damages that result from a failure of the custodian, the Investment Manager, or any other agent, representative or service provider of the Fund with
which the Fund has an existing contractual relationship to provide the services underlying the error. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>7.</B><B></B><B><U>&nbsp;Compliance</U></B>. (a)&nbsp;The <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Sub-Adviser</FONT> shall notify the Investment
Manager promptly (and, in any event, within 24 hours) upon detection of any breach of any of the Investment Guidelines, Board/Investment Manager Procedures and of any violation of any applicable law or regulation, including the 1940 Act and
Subchapter M of the Internal Revenue Code, relating to the Allocated Assets. The <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Sub-Adviser</FONT> shall also notify the Investment Manager promptly upon detection of any violations of the <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Sub-Adviser&#146;s</FONT> own compliance policies and procedures that relate to (i)&nbsp;its management of the Allocated Assets, or (ii)&nbsp;its activities as investment adviser generally to the extent such violation
could be considered material to the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Sub-Adviser&#146;s</FONT> management of the Allocated Assets or material to the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Sub-Adviser&#146;s</FONT> relevant control environment in relation
to its services for the Allocated Assets. In addition, the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Sub-Adviser</FONT> shall promptly provide the Investment Manager a memorandum of the type described in Section&nbsp;6(h). </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(b) The <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Sub-Adviser</FONT> shall provide its compliance policies and procedures (or summaries thereof)
pertaining to the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Sub-Adviser&#146;s</FONT> services provided to the Fund under this Agreement and to the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Sub-Adviser&#146;s</FONT> operations to the extent relevant to its provision
of such services to the Fund&#146;s Chief Compliance Officer to permit the Fund&#146;s Chief Compliance Officer to conduct review and oversight of such policies and procedures in accordance with Rule <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">38a-1</FONT>
under the 1940 Act and shall, on at least a quarterly basis (and, if any of the following events is reasonably likely to be material to the Fund or the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Sub-Adviser&#146;s</FONT> ability to perform its obligations
under this Agreement, promptly), notify the Investment Manager of: (i)&nbsp;any material changes to its compliance policies and procedures; (ii)&nbsp;any new policies and procedures that the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Sub-Adviser</FONT> adopts
pursuant to Rule <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">206(4)-7</FONT> under the Advisers Act or otherwise as they pertain to activities performed for or on behalf of the Fund; (iii)&nbsp;the retirement of any policies and procedures previously adopted
by the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Sub-Adviser</FONT> pursuant to Rule <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">206(4)-7</FONT> under the Advisers Act or otherwise as they pertained to activities performed for or on behalf of the Fund; and
(iv)&nbsp;any breach of its policies and procedures (A)&nbsp;as they pertain to activities performed for or on behalf of the Fund, or (B)&nbsp;that is reasonably likely to have a material adverse effect on the
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Sub-Adviser&#146;s</FONT> ability to continue to perform its obligations hereunder. The Fund, the Investment Manager, or the Fund&#146;s Chief Compliance Officer may make any reasonable request for the provision of
information or for other cooperation from the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Sub-Adviser</FONT> with respect to the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Sub-Adviser&#146;s</FONT> duties under this Agreement, and the
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Sub-Adviser</FONT> shall use its best reasonable efforts to promptly comply with such request, including without limitation furnishing the Fund, the Investment Manager, or the Fund&#146;s Chief Compliance Officer
with such documents, reports, data and other information as the Fund may reasonably request regarding transactions on behalf of the Fund, the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Sub-Adviser&#146;s</FONT> performance hereunder or compliance with the
terms hereof, and participating in such meetings (and <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">on-site</FONT> visits among representatives of the Fund and the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Sub-Adviser)</FONT> as the Fund may reasonably request from time
to time. Further, the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Sub-Adviser</FONT> shall provide the Fund&#146;s custodian with such documents, reports, data and other information as the Fund may reasonably request. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">C-9 </P>

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(c) The <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Sub-Adviser</FONT> has adopted a written code of ethics
complying with the requirements of Rule <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">17j-1</FONT> under the 1940 Act and Section&nbsp;204A of the Advisers Act and has provided the Fund with a copy of the code of ethics and evidence of its adoption, and will
notify the Fund, the Investment Manager or the Fund&#146;s Chief Compliance Officer of any material changes to (including policies added to or deleted from) its code of ethics within 30 days of the change. Within forty-five (45)&nbsp;days of the end
of the last calendar quarter of each year while this Agreement is in effect or upon the written request of the Fund, the Investment Manager, or the Fund&#146;s Chief Compliance Officer, the president or a vice president, chief compliance officer or
general partner or managing member or the equivalent of the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Sub-Adviser</FONT> shall certify to the Fund that the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Sub-Adviser</FONT> has complied with the requirement of Rule <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">17j-1</FONT> and Section&nbsp;204A during the previous year and that there have been no issues arising under its code of ethics or procedures including, but not limited to, material violations of its code or procedures,
or, if such an issue has arisen, that appropriate action was taken in response to such issue. Upon the written request of the Fund, the Investment Manager, or the Fund&#146;s Chief Compliance Officer, the
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Sub-Adviser</FONT> shall permit the Fund, the Investment Manager, and their employees or agents to examine the reports required to be made to the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Sub-Adviser</FONT> by Rule <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">17j-1(d)(1)</FONT> insofar as they relate to the Fund or as otherwise may be reasonably requested by the Fund, the Investment Manager, or the Fund&#146;s Chief Compliance Officer. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(d) The <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Sub-Adviser</FONT> has established and will keep in effect a &#147;disaster recovery&#148;
preparedness plan that sets forth procedures for recovery of critical business functions at minimum operating levels and is reasonably designed so that it can be implemented within a 24 hour time period. The

<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>8.</B><B></B><B>&nbsp;<U>Insurance</U></B>. The <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Sub-Adviser</FONT> shall maintain errors and omissions
insurance coverage and fidelity insurance coverage from insurance providers that are in the business of regularly providing insurance coverage to investment advisers. In no event shall the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Sub-Adviser&#146;s</FONT>
errors and omissions insurance coverage be less than $1&nbsp;million or the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Sub-Adviser&#146;s</FONT> fidelity insurance coverage be less than $1&nbsp;million. The <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Sub-Adviser</FONT>
shall provide prior written notice to the Investment Manager (a)&nbsp;of any material changes in its insurance policies or insurance coverage; or (b)&nbsp;if any material claims will be made on its insurance policies. Furthermore, it shall upon
request provide to the Investment Manager any information it may reasonably require concerning the amount of or scope of such insurance, provided that the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Sub-Adviser</FONT> is not obligated to provide confidential
information such as the insurance policies or claims history. The <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Sub-Adviser</FONT> has provided copies of its certificate(s) of insurance for applicable policies in effect as of the date of this Agreement,
reflecting coverage acceptable to the Investment Manager, and the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Sub-Adviser</FONT> will provide certificates of applicable insurance from time to time upon request of the Investment Manager. </P>

investment <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">sub-adviser</FONT> to fiduciary and other managed accounts including, but not limited to, investment companies and other pooled investment vehicles, and that the Investment Manager and the Trust have no

Notwithstanding the foregoing, the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Sub-Adviser</FONT> agrees that, so long as this Agreement is in effect, it shall not provide to an investment company registered under the 1940 Act investment advisory services

advice only with respect to a portion of the assets of such </P>

the form and for the period required by <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Rule&nbsp;31a-2</FONT> under the 1940 Act or such longer period as the Investment Manager or Fund may direct, all records relating to the

and regulations thereunder, and by other applicable legal provisions, including the Advisers Act, the 1934 Act, the CEA, and rules and regulations thereunder, and the Fund&#146;s compliance policies and procedures, and to preserve such records for
the periods and in the manner required by that Section, and those rules, regulations, legal provisions and compliance policies and procedures. In compliance with the requirements of Rule <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">31a-3</FONT> under the 1940
Act, any records required to be maintained and preserved pursuant to the provisions of <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Rule&nbsp;31a-1</FONT> and <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Rule&nbsp;31a-2</FONT> promulgated under the 1940 Act which are
prepared or maintained by the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Sub-Adviser</FONT> on behalf of the Fund are the property of the Fund and shall be surrendered promptly to the Fund or the Investment Manager on request except to the extent that copies
are retained by the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Sub-Adviser</FONT> in furtherance of its own record retention policies. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(b) The <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Sub-Adviser</FONT> agrees that all accounts, books and other records maintained and preserved by it on behalf of the Fund as required hereby shall be subject at any time, and from time to time, to such periodic, special
and other examinations by the Securities and Exchange Commission, the Fund&#146;s auditors, the Fund or any representative of the Fund (including, without limitation, the Fund&#146;s Chief Compliance Officer), the Investment Manager, or any
governmental agency or other instrumentality having regulatory authority over the Investment Manager or the Fund. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>13.</B><B></B><B>&nbsp;<U>Reference to the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Sub-Adviser</FONT></U></B>. The Investment Manager and the
Trust are authorized to publish and distribute any information, including but not limited to registration statements, advertising or promotional material, regarding the provision of <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">sub-investment</FONT> advisory
services by the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Sub-Adviser</FONT> pursuant to this Agreement and to use in advertising, publicity or otherwise the name of the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Sub-Adviser,</FONT> or any trade name, trademark, trade
device, service mark, symbol or logo of the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Sub-Adviser,</FONT> without the prior written consent of the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Sub-Adviser.</FONT> In addition, the Investment Manager may distribute
information regarding the provision of <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">sub-investment</FONT> advisory services by the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Sub-Adviser</FONT> to the Board without the prior written consent of the <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Sub-Adviser.</FONT> The Investment Manager shall provide final copies of such items to the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Sub-Adviser</FONT> upon request within a reasonable time following such use, publication or
distribution. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>14.</B><B></B><B>&nbsp;<U>Standard of Care, Liability and Indemnification</U></B>. (a)&nbsp;The <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Sub-Adviser</FONT> shall fully and faithfully discharge all its obligations, duties and responsibilities pursuant to this Agreement, (i)&nbsp;solely in the best interest of the Fund and its shareholders, (ii)&nbsp;in good
faith and with the due care, skill, prudence, and diligence under the circumstances then prevailing that a prudent, professional fiduciary investment adviser acting in a like capacity, would use in the conduct of an enterprise of a like character
and with like aims, and (iii)&nbsp;otherwise in accordance with documents and instruments governing the Fund. For the avoidance of doubt, the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Sub-Adviser</FONT> shall not deliberately use any procedure in discharging
its obligations hereunder that it believes is inferior to the procedures employed by it for any other similarly situated account for which the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Sub-Adviser</FONT> or any of its advisory affiliates discharge
obligations (either alone or in conjunction with others) similar to those undertaken by the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Sub-Adviser</FONT> hereunder, except if there is a good faith basis, consistent with the standard of care under this
Section&nbsp;14(a), for the use of the procedure. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(b) The <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Sub-Adviser</FONT> shall not be liable for any
losses, claims, damages, liabilities or litigation (including legal and other expenses) incurred or suffered by the Investment Manager or the Trust or any of the Investment Manager Indemnitees (as defined below) as a result of any error of judgment
by the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Sub-Adviser</FONT> with respect to the Fund, except as may otherwise be provided by the 1940 Act or any other federal securities or commodities </P>

<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>15.</B><B></B><B>&nbsp;<U>Duration and Termination</U></B>. (a)&nbsp;This Agreement is effective as of the Effective Date, and shall
continue in full force and effect with respect to the Fund until 2 years from the Effective Date; provided that this Agreement shall continue in full force and effect with respect to the Fund from year to year thereafter so long as such continuance
is specifically approved at least annually (i)&nbsp;by the vote of a majority of those Trustees of the Trust who are not parties to this Agreement or interested persons of any such party, cast in person at a meeting called for the purpose of voting
on such approval, and (ii)&nbsp;by either the vote of (A)&nbsp;the Board or (B)&nbsp;a majority of the outstanding voting securities of the Fund (within the meaning of the 1940 Act); provided further, that if the shareholders fail to approve the
Agreement as provided herein, the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Sub-Adviser</FONT> may continue to serve hereunder in the manner and to the extent permitted by the 1940 Act and the rules and regulations thereunder. The foregoing requirement that
continuance of this Agreement be &#147;specifically approved at least annually&#148; shall be construed in a manner consistent with the 1940 Act and the rules and regulations thereunder. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(b) This Agreement may be terminated at any time, without the payment of any penalty, (i)&nbsp;by vote of a majority of the Board or by a vote
of a majority of the outstanding voting securities of the Fund; (ii)&nbsp;by the Investment Manager on not less than 60 days written notice to the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Sub-Adviser</FONT> (or immediately in the event of a material breach
by the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Sub-Adviser),</FONT> or (iii)&nbsp;by the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Sub-Adviser</FONT> on not less than 90 days written notice to the Investment Manager and the Trust. Notwithstanding the above, the <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Sub-Adviser</FONT> may not terminate the Agreement during the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">24-month</FONT> period immediately following the Effective Date. This Agreement shall automatically terminate in the event of
its assignment or the assignment of the Management Agreement. This Agreement shall also terminate in the event that the Management Agreement by and between the Trust on behalf of the Fund and the Investment Manager referred to in Section&nbsp;1 is
terminated and the Investment Manager shall notify the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Sub-Adviser</FONT> promptly after receiving any notice relating to the termination of such Management Agreement. In the event of termination for any reason, all
records of the Fund that are maintained by the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Sub-Adviser</FONT> in accordance with the 1940 Act and Section&nbsp;12 of this Agreement shall, upon written request from the Investment Manager or the Trust, promptly
be returned to the Investment Manager or the Trust, free from any claim or retention of rights in such records by the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Sub-Adviser,</FONT> although the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Sub-Adviser</FONT> may, at its
expense, make and retain a copy of such records. This Agreement may be terminated with respect to one or more series of the Trust listed on Annex A without affecting the continuity, validity or enforceability of this Agreement with respect to any
other series of the Trust listed on Annex A. Promptly following the termination of this Agreement with respect to any series of the Trust listed on Annex A, Annex A shall be amended to remove references to such series of the Trust. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(c) Unless otherwise provided in this Agreement or otherwise agreed by the Investment Manager in writing, all notices and other communications
hereunder shall be in writing. Notices and other writings delivered or mailed postage prepaid to the Investment Manager and the Trust at 200 West Street, New York, New York 10282, Attention: Caroline Kraus, Esq., or to the <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Sub-Adviser</FONT> at CoreCommodity Management, LLC, 680 Washington Blvd., 11<SUP STYLE="font-size:85%; vertical-align:top">th</SUP> Floor, Stamford, CT 06901 and to Legal@CoreCommodityLLC.com, or to such other address as
the Investment Manager or the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Sub-Adviser</FONT> may hereafter specify by written notice to the most recent address specified by the other party, shall be deemed to have been properly delivered or given hereunder to
the respective addressee. </P>
